        });

        <!-- BEGIN Redirect old post id anchors -->
        <script>
	var anchor = window.location.hash.match(/^#(post|p|msg|entry)(\d+)$/);
	if (anchor && anchor.length === 3) {
		var redirectAnchor = 'post-' + anchor[2];
		// if we have an anchor on the page, simply jump to the anchor
		if (document.getElementById(redirectAnchor) != null) {
			window.location.hash = redirectAnchor;
		} else {
			window.location.href = "/posts/" + anchor[2];
		}
	}
        </script>
        <!-- END Redirect old post id anchors -->
